;;;; Define Nat
  (: Nat Type)
  (: Z Nat)
  (: S 
    (-> Nat Nat))
;;;; Define <=
  (: <= 
    (-> $a $a Bool))
  (= 
    (<= $x $y) 
    (or 
      (< $x $y) 
      (== $x $y)))
;;;; Define cast functions between Nat and Number
  (: fromNumber 
    (-> Number Nat))
  (= 
    (fromNumber $n) 
    (if 
      (<= $n 0) Z 
      (S (fromNumber (- $n 1)))))
  (: fromNat 
    (-> Nat Number))
  (= 
    (fromNat Z) 0)
  (= 
    (fromNat (S $k)) 
    (+ 1 
      (fromNat $k)))
